# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 01:35:55.097645

### Base Program

```py
def pillowHolder(n, time):
    time %= (2 * n - 2)
    if time <= n - 1:
        return time + 1
    else:
        return 2 * n - time - 1
```

### Input

```json
[42, 1]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def pillowHolder(n, time):
    time %= 2 * n - 2
    if time <= n - 1:
        return time + 1
    else:
        return 2 * n - time - 1
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def pillowHolder(var_0, var_1):
    var_1 %= 2 * var_0 - 2
    if var_1 <= var_0 - 1:
        return var_1 + 1
    else:
        return 2 * var_0 - var_1 - 1
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def pillowHolder(n, time):
    time %= n * 2 + -2
    if time <= n + -1:
        return 1 + time
    else:
        return n * 2 + -time + -1
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def pillowHolder(var_2, var_3):
    var_3 %= var_2 * 2 + -2
    if var_3 <= var_2 + -1:
        return 1 + var_3
    else:
        return var_2 * 2 + -var_3 + -1
```
